SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)

SELECT `m`.`id`, `m`.`album`, `m`.`alias`, `m`.`artist`, `m`.`category`, `m`.`created_at`, `m`.`deleted_at`, `m`.`is_active`, `m`.`is_deleted`, `m`.`is_requestable`, `m`.`last_sung_at`, `m`.`lyrics_url`, `m`.`mr_url`, `m`.`pitch`, `m`.`proficiency`, `m`.`reference_url`, `m`.`required_points`, `m`.`sing_count`, `m`.`song_library_id`, `m`.`streamer_profile_id`, `m`.`thumbnail_path`, `m`.`thumbnail_url`, `m`.`title`, `m`.`title_chosung`, `m`.`title_vector`, `m`.`updated_at`
FROM (

                        SELECT * FROM func_song_books
                        WHERE streamer_profile_id = @p0 AND is_active = 1 AND is_deleted = 0
                        ORDER BY VEC_DISTANCE_COSINE(title_vector, VEC_FromText(@p1))
                        LIMIT @p2
) AS `m`
WHERE NOT (`m`.`is_deleted`)
